<h2 id="anatomy" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Anatomy</h2>

<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<h3 id="basic" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#basic"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Basic</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Set up a basic image cropper. Drag the handles to resize the selection, or drag inside to pan the image.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="aspect-ratio" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#aspect-ratio"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Aspect Ratio</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Lock the crop area to a specific aspect ratio. Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">aspectRatio</code> prop—pass a number like <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">16/9</code> for widescreen or
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">1</code> for square.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8lhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8lhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8lhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="circle-crop" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#circle-crop"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Circle Crop</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">cropShape=&quot;circle&quot;</code> for profile pictures or avatars. The selection becomes a circle instead of a rectangle.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8rhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8rhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8rhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="initial-crop" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#initial-crop"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Initial Crop</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Start with a pre-defined crop area using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">initialCrop</code> prop. Pass an object with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">x</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">y</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">width</code>, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">height</code> in
pixels.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_91hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_91hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_91hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled-zoom" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled-zoom"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled Zoom</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Control zoom programmatically with the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">zoom</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onZoomChange</code> props. Useful when you want external buttons to zoom in
and out.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_97hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_97hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_97hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="zoom-limits" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#zoom-limits"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Zoom Limits</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Set <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">minZoom</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maxZoom</code> to constrain how far users can zoom. Prevents over-zooming or zooming out past the image
bounds.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9dhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="rotation" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#rotation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Rotation</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Rotate the image with the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">rotation</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onRotationChange</code> props. Values are in degrees—common increments are 90
or 180.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9jhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="flip" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#flip"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Flip</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Flip the image horizontally or vertically using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">flip</code> prop. Pass an object with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">horizontal</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">vertical</code>
booleans.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="min-and-max-size" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#min-and-max-size"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Min and Max Size</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Constrain the crop area size with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">minWidth</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">minHeight</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maxWidth</code>, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maxHeight</code>. Keeps the selection within
sensible bounds.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="fixed-crop-area" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#fixed-crop-area"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Fixed Crop Area</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Set <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">fixedCropArea</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code> when the crop area should stay fixed while the image moves underneath. Useful for
overlay-style cropping.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a5hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a5hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a5hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="crop-preview" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#crop-preview"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Crop Preview</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">getCroppedImage()</code> from the context to get the cropped result. Call it with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">{ output: &#x27;dataUrl&#x27; }</code> for a base64
string you can use in an <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">img</code> src.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_abhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_abhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_abhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="reset" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#reset"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Reset</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The context exposes a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">reset()</code> method that restores the image to its initial state. Handy for an &quot;undo&quot; or &quot;start over&quot;
button.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_ahhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_ahhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_ahhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="events" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Events</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Listen to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onCropChange</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onZoomChange</code> to track crop position and zoom level. Use these to sync with external state
or show live previews.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_anhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_anhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_anhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ImageCropper.Context</code> to access the cropper API from anywhere inside the root. You get methods like <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">zoomBy</code>,
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">rotateBy</code>, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">setZoom</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_athanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_athanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_athanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useImageCropper</code> when you need to control the cropper from outside the component tree. Build
custom toolbars or integrate with form state.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_b3hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_b3hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_b3hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><p class="text c_fg.muted">Renders a <code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&lt;div&gt;</code> element.</p><div Pass a boolean to set explicitly or omit to toggle.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">resize</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(handlePosition: HandlePosition, delta: number) =&gt; void</code><p class="text">Function to resize the crop area from a handle programmatically.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">reset</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">() =&gt; void</code><p class="text">Function to reset the cropper to its initial state.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">getCroppedImage</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(options?: GetCroppedImageOptions) =&gt; Promise&lt;string | Blob&gt;</code><p class="text">Function to get the cropped image with all transformations applied.
Returns a Promise that resolves to either a Blob or data URL.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">getCropData</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">() =&gt; CropData</code><p class="text">Function to get the crop data in natural image pixel coordinates.
These coordinates are relative to the original image dimensions,
accounting for zoom, rotation, and flip transformations.
Use this for server-side cropping or state persistence.</p></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div></article><div class="d_flex flex-d_column-reverse sm:flex-d_row jc_space-between gap_3"><a /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"image-cropper\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cImageCropper.Root\u003e\n  \u003cImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Image /\u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Handle /\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Grid /\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n  \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n\u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n### Basic\n\nSet up a basic image cropper. Drag the handles to resize the selection, or drag inside to pan the image.\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Basic = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport styles from \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            class={styles.Image}\n      \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport styles \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Aspect Ratio\n\nLock the crop area to a specific aspect ratio. Use the `aspectRatio` prop—pass a number like `16/9` for widescreen or\n`1` for square.\n\n**Example: aspect-ratio**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport { RectangleHorizontalIcon, SquareIcon, RectangleVerticalIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nconst aspects = [\n  { label: '16:9', value: 16 / 9, icon: RectangleHorizontalIcon },\n  { label: '1:1', value: 1, icon: SquareIcon },\n  { label: '9:16', value: 9 / 16, icon: RectangleVerticalIcon },\n]\n\nexport const AspectRatio = () =\u003e {\n  const [aspectRatio, setAspectRatio] = useState(16 / 9)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={button.Group}\u003e\n        {aspects.map((aspect) =\u003e (\n          \u003cbutton\n            key={aspect.label}\n            className={button.Root}\n            data-variant={aspectRatio === aspect.value ? 'solid' : undefined}\n            onClick={() =\u003e setAspectRatio(aspect.value)}\n          \u003e\n            \u003caspect.icon /\u003e\n            {aspect.label}\n          \u003c/button\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root className={styles.Root} aspectRatio={aspectRatio}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport { RectangleHorizontalIcon, SquareIcon, RectangleVerticalIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nconst aspects = [\n  { label: '16:9', value: 16 / 9, icon: RectangleHorizontalIcon },\n  { label: '1:1', value: 1, icon: SquareIcon },\n  { label: '9:16', value: 9 / 16, icon: RectangleVerticalIcon },\n]\n\nexport const AspectRatio = () =\u003e {\n  const [aspectRatio, setAspectRatio] = createSignal(16 / 9)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cFor each={aspects}\u003e\n          {(aspect) =\u003e (\n            \u003cbutton\n              class={button.Root}\n              data-variant={aspectRatio() === aspect.value ? 'solid' : undefined}\n              onClick={() =\u003e setAspectRatio(aspect.value)}\n            \u003e\n              \u003caspect.icon /\u003e\n              {aspect.label}\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/For\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root} aspectRatio={aspectRatio()}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            class={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport { RectangleHorizontal, Square, RectangleVertical } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref, markRaw } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nconst aspects = [\n  { label: '16:9', value: 16 / 9, icon: markRaw(RectangleHorizontal) },\n  { label: '1:1', value: 1, icon: markRaw(Square) },\n  { label: '9:16', value: 9 / 16, icon: markRaw(RectangleVertical) },\n]\n\nconst aspectRatio = ref(16 / 9)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Layout\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"button.Group\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        v-for=\"aspect in aspects\"\n        :key=\"aspect.label\"\n        :class=\"button.Root\"\n        :data-variant=\"aspectRatio === aspect.value ? 'solid' : undefined\"\n        @click=\"aspectRatio = aspect.value\"\n      \u003e\n        \u003ccomponent :is=\"aspect.icon\" /\u003e\n        {{ aspect.label }}\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cImageCropper.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :aspectRatio=\"aspectRatio\"\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Viewport :class=\"styles.Viewport\"\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Image\n          :class=\"styles.Image\"\n          src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n          alt=\"Sample\"\n        /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Selection :class=\"styles.Selection\"\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle\n            v-for=\"position in ImageCropper.handles\"\n            :key=\"position\"\n            :class=\"styles.Handle\"\n            :position=\"position\"\n          \u003e\n            \u003cdiv /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/svelte/image-cropper'\n  import { RectangleHorizontalIcon, SquareIcon, RectangleVerticalIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\n  const aspects = [\n    { label: '16:9', value: 16 / 9, icon: RectangleHorizontalIcon },\n    { label: '1:1', value: 1, icon: SquareIcon },\n    { label: '9:16', value: 9 / 16, icon: RectangleVerticalIcon },\n  ]\n\n  let aspectRatio = $state(16 / 9)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n    {#each aspects as aspect}\n      \u003cbutton\n        type=\"button\"\n        class={button.Root}\n        data-variant={aspectRatio === aspect.value ? 'solid' : undefined}\n        onclick={() =\u003e (aspectRatio = aspect.value)}\n      \u003e\n        \u003caspect.icon /\u003e\n        {aspect.label}\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root} {aspectRatio}\u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Image\n        class={styles.Image}\n        src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n        alt=\"Sample\"\n      /\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n        {#each ImageCropper.handles as position}\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} {position}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n        {/each}\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Circle Crop\n\nUse `cropShape=\"circle\"` for profile pictures or avatars. The selection becomes a circle instead of a rectangle.\n\n**Example: circle**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Circle = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root className={styles.Root} cropShape=\"circle\"\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Circle = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root} cropShape=\"circle\"\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            class={styles.Image}\n      \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Layout\"\u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" \u003cImageCropper.Handle\n            v-for=\"position in ImageCropper.handles\"\n            :key=\"position\"\n            :class=\"styles.Handle\"\n            :position=\"position\"\n          \u003e\n            \u003cdiv /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/svelte/image-cropper'\n  import styles from the `initialCrop` prop. Pass an object with `x`, `y`, `width`, and `height` in\npixels.\n\n**Example: initial-crop**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const InitialCrop = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cp className={styles.Description}\u003eStarts with a pre-defined crop area\u003c/p\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root className={styles.Root} initialCrop={{ x: 50, y: 30, width: 200, height: 120 }}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For } from      \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled Zoom\n\nControl zoom programmatically with the `zoom` and `onZoomChange` props. Useful when you want external buttons to zoom in\nand out.\n\n**Example: controlled-zoom**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const ControlledZoom = () =\u003e {\n  const [zoom, setZoom] = useState(1)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setZoom(zoom - 0.1)}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cspan style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', minWidth: '3rem', textAlign: 'center' }}\u003e{zoom.toFixed(1)}x\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setZoom(zoom + 0.1)}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root className={styles.Root} zoom={zoom} onZoomChange={(e) =\u003e setZoom(e.zoom)}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const ControlledZoom = () =\u003e {\n  const [zoom, setZoom] = createSignal(1)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setZoom(zoom() - 0.1)}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cspan style={{ 'font-size': '0.875rem', 'min-width': '3rem', 'text-align': 'center' }}\u003e\n          {zoom().toFixed(1)}x\n        \u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setZoom(zoom() + 0.1)}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root} zoom={zoom()} onZoomChange={(e) =\u003e setZoom(e.zoom)}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            class={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomIn, ZoomOut } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nconst zoom = ref(1)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Layout\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"button.Group\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"zoom -= 0.1\"\u003e\n        \u003cZoomOut /\u003e\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cspan :style=\"{ fontSize: '0.875rem', minWidth: '3rem', textAlign: 'center' }\"\u003e{{ zoom.toFixed(1) }}x\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"zoom += 0.1\"\u003e\n        \u003cZoomIn /\u003e\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cImageCropper.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-model:zoom=\"zoom\"\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Viewport :class=\"styles.Viewport\"\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Image\n          :class=\"styles.Image\"\n          src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n          alt=\"Sample\"\n        /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Selection :class=\"styles.Selection\"\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle\n            v-for=\"position in ImageCropper.handles\"\n            :key=\"position\"\n            :class=\"styles.Handle\"\n            :position=\"position\"\n          \u003e\n            \u003cdiv /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/svelte/image-cropper'\n  import { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\n  let zoom = $state(1)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e (zoom -= 0.1)}\u003e\n      \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cspan style=\"font-size: 0.875rem; min-width: 3rem; text-align: center;\"\u003e{zoom.toFixed(1)}x\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e (zoom += 0.1)}\u003e\n      \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root} bind:zoom\u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Image\n        class={styles.Image}\n        src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n        alt=\"Sample\"\n      /\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n        {#each ImageCropper.handles as position}\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} {position}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n        {/each}\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Zoom Limits\n\nSet `minZoom` and `maxZoom` to constrain how far users can zoom. Prevents over-zooming or zooming out past the image\nbounds.\n\n**Example: zoom-limits**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const ZoomLimits = () =\u003e {\n  const [zoom, setZoom] = useState(1)\n  const minZoom = 0.5\n  const maxZoom = 2\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setZoom(Math.max(minZoom, zoom - 0.1))}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cspan style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', padding: '0 0.5rem', minWidth: '3rem', textAlign: 'center' }}\u003e\n          {zoom.toFixed(1)}x\n        \u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setZoom(Math.min(maxZoom, zoom + 0.1))}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cp className={styles.Description}\u003e\n        Zoom constrained between {minZoom}x and {maxZoom}x\n      \u003c/p\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root\n        className={styles.Root}\n        zoom={zoom}\n        onZoomChange={(e) =\u003e setZoom(e.zoom)}\n        minZoom={minZoom}\n        maxZoom={maxZoom}\n      \u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const ZoomLimits = () =\u003e {\n  const [zoom, setZoom] = createSignal(1)\n  const minZoom = 0.5\n  const maxZoom = 2\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setZoom(Math.max(minZoom, zoom() - 0.1))}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cspan style={{ 'font-size': '0.875rem', padding: '0 0.5rem', 'min-width': '3rem', 'text-align': 'center' }}\u003e\n          {zoom().toFixed(1)}x\n        \u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setZoom(Math.min(maxZoom, zoom() + 0.1))}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cp class={styles.Description}\u003e\n        Zoom constrained between {minZoom}x and {maxZoom}x\n      \u003c/p\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root\n        class={styles.Root}\n        zoom={zoom()}\n        onZoomChange={(e) =\u003e setZoom(e.zoom)}\n        minZoom={minZoom}\n        maxZoom={maxZoom}\n      \u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            class={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomIn, ZoomOut } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nconst zoom = ref(1)\nconst minZoom = 0.5\nconst maxZoom = 2\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Layout\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"button.Group\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"zoom = Math.max(minZoom, zoom - 0.1)\"\u003e\n        \u003cZoomOut /\u003e\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cspan :style=\"{ fontSize: '0.875rem', padding: '0 0.5rem', minWidth: '3rem', textAlign: 'center' }\"\u003e\n        {{ zoom.toFixed(1) }}x\n      \u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"zoom = Math.min(maxZoom, zoom + 0.1)\"\u003e\n        \u003cZoomIn /\u003e\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cp :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003eZoom constrained between {{ minZoom }}x and {{ maxZoom }}x\u003c/p\u003e\n\n    \u003cImageCropper.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-model:zoom=\"zoom\" :minZoom=\"minZoom\" :maxZoom=\"maxZoom\"\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Viewport :class=\"styles.Viewport\"\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Image\n          :class=\"styles.Image\"\n          src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n          alt=\"Sample\"\n        /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Selection :class=\"styles.Selection\"\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle\n            v-for=\"position in ImageCropper.handles\"\n            :key=\"position\"\n            :class=\"styles.Handle\"\n            :position=\"position\"\n          \u003e\n            \u003cdiv /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/svelte/image-cropper'\n  import { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\n  let zoom = $state(1)\n  const minZoom = 0.5\n  const maxZoom = 2\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e (zoom = Math.max(minZoom, zoom - 0.1))}\u003e\n      \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cspan style=\"font-size: 0.875rem; padding: 0 0.5rem; min-width: 3rem; text-align: center;\"\u003e\n      {zoom.toFixed(1)}x\n    \u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e (zoom = Math.min(maxZoom, zoom + 0.1))}\u003e\n      \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cp class={styles.Description}\u003eZoom constrained between {minZoom}x and {maxZoom}x\u003c/p\u003e\n\n  \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root} bind:zoom {minZoom} {maxZoom}\u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Image\n        class={styles.Image}\n        src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n        alt=\"Sample\"\n      /\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n        {#each ImageCropper.handles as position}\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} {position}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n        {/each}\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Rotation\n\nRotate the image with the `rotation` and `onRotationChange` props. Values are in degrees—common increments are 90\nor 180.\n\n**Example: rotation**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon, RotateCwIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Rotation = () =\u003e {\n  const [rotation, setRotation] = useState(0)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setRotation(rotation - 90)}\u003e\n          \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setRotation(rotation + 90)}\u003e\n          \u003cRotateCwIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cspan style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', padding: '0 0.5rem' }}\u003e{rotation}°\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root className={styles.Root} rotation={rotation} onRotationChange={(e) =\u003e setRotation(e.rotation)}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport { RotateCcwIcon, RotateCwIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Rotation = () =\u003e {\n  const [rotation, setRotation] = createSignal(0)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setRotation(rotation() - 90)}\u003e\n          \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e setRotation(rotation() + 90)}\u003e\n          \u003cRotateCwIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cspan style={{ 'font-size': '0.875rem', padding: '0 0.5rem' }}\u003e{rotation()}deg\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root} rotation={rotation()} onRotationChange={(e) =\u003e setRotation(e.rotation)}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            class={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport { RotateCcw, RotateCw } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nconst rotation = ref(0)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Layout\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"button.Group\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"rotation -= 90\"\u003e\n        \u003cRotateCcw /\u003e\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"rotation += 90\"\u003e\n        \u003cRotateCw /\u003e\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cspan :style=\"{ fontSize: '0.875rem', padding: '0 0.5rem' }\"\u003e{{ rotation }}deg\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cImageCropper.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :rotation=\"rotation\" @rotation-change=\"(e) =\u003e (rotation = e.rotation)\"\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Viewport :class=\"styles.Viewport\"\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Image\n          :class=\"styles.Image\"\n          src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n          alt=\"Sample\"\n        /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Selection :class=\"styles.Selection\"\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle\n            v-for=\"position in ImageCropper.handles\"\n            :key=\"position\"\n            :class=\"styles.Handle\"\n            :position=\"position\"\n          \u003e\n            \u003cdiv /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/svelte/image-cropper'\n  import { RotateCcwIcon, RotateCwIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\n  let rotation = $state(0)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e (rotation -= 90)}\u003e\n      \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e (rotation += 90)}\u003e\n      \u003cRotateCwIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cspan style=\"font-size: 0.875rem; padding: 0 0.5rem;\"\u003e{rotation}deg\u003c/span\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root} {rotation} onRotationChange={(e) =\u003e (rotation = e.rotation)}\u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Image\n        class={styles.Image}\n        src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n        alt=\"Sample\"\n      /\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Selection
