\u003cdiv\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n        {/each}\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Flip\n\nFlip the image horizontally or vertically using the `flip` prop. Pass an object with `horizontal` and `vertical`\nbooleans.\n\n**Example: flip**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport { FlipHorizontalIcon, FlipVerticalIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Flip = () =\u003e {\n  const [flip, setFlip] = useState({ horizontal: false, vertical: false })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          className={button.Root}\n          data-variant={flip.horizontal ? 'solid' : undefined}\n          onClick={() =\u003e setFlip({ ...flip, horizontal: !flip.horizontal })}\n        \u003e\n          \u003cFlipHorizontalIcon /\u003e\n          Horizontal\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          className={button.Root}\n          data-variant={flip.vertical ? 'solid' : undefined}\n          onClick={() =\u003e setFlip({ ...flip, vertical: !flip.vertical })}\n        \u003e\n          \u003cFlipVerticalIcon /\u003e\n          Vertical\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root className={styles.Root} flip={flip} onFlipChange={(e) =\u003e setFlip(e.flip)}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport { FlipHorizontalIcon, FlipVerticalIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Flip = () =\u003e {\n  const [flip, setFlip] = createSignal({ horizontal: false, vertical: false })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          class={button.Root}\n          data-variant={flip().horizontal ? 'solid' : undefined}\n          onClick={() =\u003e setFlip({ ...flip(), horizontal: !flip().horizontal })}\n        \u003e\n          \u003cFlipHorizontalIcon /\u003e\n          Horizontal\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton\n          class={button.Root}\n          data-variant={flip().vertical ? 'solid' : undefined}\n          onClick={() =\u003e setFlip({ ...flip(), vertical: !flip().vertical })}\n        \u003e\n          \u003cFlipVerticalIcon /\u003e\n          Vertical\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root} flip={flip()} onFlipChange={(e) =\u003e setFlip(e.flip)}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            class={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport { FlipHorizontal, FlipVertical } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nconst flip = ref({ horizontal: false, vertical: false })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Layout\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"button.Group\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        :class=\"button.Root\"\n        :data-variant=\"flip.horizontal ? 'solid' : undefined\"\n        @click=\"flip = { ...flip, horizontal: !flip.horizontal }\"\n      \u003e\n        \u003cFlipHorizontal /\u003e\n        Horizontal\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cbutton\n        :class=\"button.Root\"\n        :data-variant=\"flip.vertical ? 'solid' : undefined\"\n        @click=\"flip = { ...flip, vertical: !flip.vertical }\"\n      \u003e\n        \u003cFlipVertical /\u003e\n        Vertical\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cImageCropper.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :flip=\"flip\" @flip-change=\"(e) =\u003e (flip = e.flip)\"\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Viewport :class=\"styles.Viewport\"\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Image\n          :class=\"styles.Image\"\n          src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n          alt=\"Sample\"\n        /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Selection :class=\"styles.Selection\"\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle\n            v-for=\"position in ImageCropper.handles\"\n            :key=\"position\"\n            :class=\"styles.Handle\"\n            :position=\"position\"\n          \u003e\n            \u003cdiv /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/svelte/image-cropper'\n  import { FlipHorizontalIcon, FlipVerticalIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\n  let flip = $state({ horizontal: false, vertical: false })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n    \u003cbutton\n      type=\"button\"\n      class={button.Root}\n      data-variant={flip.horizontal ? 'solid' : undefined}\n      onclick={() =\u003e (flip = { ...flip, horizontal: !flip.horizontal })}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cFlipHorizontalIcon /\u003e\n      Horizontal\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cbutton\n      type=\"button\"\n      class={button.Root}\n      data-variant={flip.vertical ? 'solid' : undefined}\n      onclick={() =\u003e (flip = { ...flip, vertical: !flip.vertical })}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cFlipVerticalIcon /\u003e\n      Vertical\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root} {flip} onFlipChange={(e) =\u003e (flip = e.flip)}\u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Image\n        class={styles.Image}\n        src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n        alt=\"Sample\"\n      /\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n        {#each ImageCropper.handles as position}\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} {position}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n        {/each}\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Min and Max Size\n\nConstrain the crop area size with `minWidth`, `minHeight`, `maxWidth`, and `maxHeight`. Keeps the selection within\nsensible bounds.\n\n**Example: min-max-size**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const MinMaxSize = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cp className={styles.Description}\u003eCrop area constrained to min 80px and max 200px\u003c/p\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root className={styles.Root} minWidth={80} minHeight={80} maxWidth={200} maxHeight={200}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport styles from crop area should stay fixed while the image moves underneath. Useful for\noverlay-style cropping.\n\n**Example: fixed**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Fixed = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root className={styles.Root} fixedCropArea\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport {          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript Call it with `{ output: 'dataUrl' }` for a base64\nstring you can use in an `img` src.\n\n**Example: crop-preview**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper, useImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport { CropIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const CropPreview = () =\u003e {\n  const imageCropper = useImageCropper()\n  const [preview, setPreview] = useState\u003cstring | null\u003e(null)\n\n  const handleCrop = async () =\u003e {\n    const result = await imageCropper.getCroppedImage({ output: 'dataUrl' })\n    if (typeof result === 'string') {\n      setPreview(result)\n    }\n  }\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\" onClick={handleCrop}\u003e\n          \u003cCropIcon /\u003e\n          Crop Image\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={imageCropper}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n            crossOrigin=\"anonymous\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.RootProvider\u003e\n\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.Preview}\u003e\n        \u003cspan className={styles.PreviewLabel}\u003ePreview\u003c/span\u003e\n        {preview \u0026\u0026 \u003cimg src={preview} alt=\"Cropped preview\" className={styles.PreviewImage} /\u003e}\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For, createSignal, Show } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper, useImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport { CropIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const CropPreview \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={imageCropper}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            class={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" ImageCropper, useImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport { Crop } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nconst imageCropper = useImageCropper()\nconst preview = ref\u003cstring | null\u003e(null)\n\nconst handleCrop = async () =\u003e {\n  const result = await v-for=\"position in ImageCropper.handles\"\n            :key=\"position\"\n            :class=\"styles.Handle\"\n            :position=\"position\"\n          \u003e\n            \u003cdiv /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\" axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.RootProvider\u003e\n\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Preview\"\u003e\n      \u003cspan :class=\"styles.PreviewLabel\"\u003ePreview\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003cimg v-if=\"preview\" :src=\"preview\" alt=\"Cropped preview\" :class=\"styles.PreviewImage\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ImageCropper, useImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/svelte/image-cropper'\n  import { CropIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\n  const imageCropper = useImageCropper()\n  let preview = $state\u003cstring | null\u003e(null)\n\n  const handleCrop = async () =\u003e {\n    const result = await imageCropper().getCroppedImage({ output: 'dataUrl' })\n    if (typeof result === 'string') {\n      preview = result\n    }\n  }\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\" onclick={handleCrop}\u003e\n      \u003cCropIcon /\u003e\n      Crop Image\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cImageCropper.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={imageCropper}\u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Image\n        class={styles.Image}\n        src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n        alt=\"Sample\"\n        crossorigin=\"anonymous\"\n      /\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n        {#each ImageCropper.handles as position}\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} {position}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n        {/each}\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003c/ImageCropper.RootProvider\u003e\n\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.Preview}\u003e\n    \u003cspan class={styles.PreviewLabel}\u003ePreview\u003c/span\u003e\n    {#if preview}\n      \u003cimg src={preview} alt=\"Cropped preview\" class={styles.PreviewImage} /\u003e\n    {/if}\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Reset\n\nThe context exposes a `reset()` method that restores the image to its initial state. Handy for an \"undo\" or \"start over\"\nbutton.\n\n**Example: reset**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper, useImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport { FlipHorizontalIcon, RotateCwIcon, RotateCcwIcon, RefreshCwIcon, ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Reset = () =\u003e {\n  const imageCropper = useImageCropper()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e imageCropper.zoomBy(-0.1)}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e imageCropper.zoomBy(0.1)}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e imageCropper.rotateBy(-90)}\u003e\n          \u003cRotateCcwIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e imageCropper.rotateBy(90)}\u003e\n          \u003cRotateCwIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e imageCropper.flipHorizontally()}\u003e\n          \u003cFlipHorizontalIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} data-variant=\"surface\" onClick={() =\u003e imageCropper.reset()}\u003e\n          \u003cRefreshCwIcon /\u003e\n          Reset\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={imageCropper}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper, \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" \u003c/ImageCropper.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper, useImageCropper } from        {/each}\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n `onZoomChange` to track crop position and zoom level. Use these to sync with external state\nor show live previews.\n\n**Example: events**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Events = () =\u003e {\n  const [cropData, setCropData] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0, width: 0, height: 0 })\n  const [zoom, setZoom] = useState(1)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root\n        className={styles.Root}\n        onCropChange={(e) =\u003e setCropData(e.crop)}\n        onZoomChange={(e) =\u003e setZoom(e.zoom)}\n      \u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.DataDisplay}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv className={styles.DataItem}\u003e\n          \u003cspan className={styles.DataLabel}\u003eZoom\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003cspan className={styles.DataValue}\u003e{zoom.toFixed(2)}x\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003cdiv className={styles.DataItem}\u003e\n          \u003cspan className={styles.DataLabel}\u003ePosition\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003cspan className={styles.DataValue}\u003e\n            {Math.round(cropData.x)}, {Math.round(cropData.y)}\n          \u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003cdiv className={styles.DataItem}\u003e\n          \u003cspan className={styles.DataLabel}\u003eSize\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003cspan className={styles.DataValue}\u003e\n            {Math.round(cropData.width)} × {Math.round(cropData.height)}\n          \u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Events = () =\u003e {\n  const [cropData, setCropData] = createSignal({ x: 0, y: 0, width: 0, height: 0 })\n  const [zoom, setZoom] = createSignal(1)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root\n        class={styles.Root}\n        onCropChange={(e)           class={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\n      \u003cdiv class={styles.DataDisplay}\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.DataItem}\u003e\n          \u003cspan class={styles.DataLabel}\u003eZoom\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003cspan class={styles.DataValue}\u003e{zoom().toFixed(2)}x\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.DataItem}\u003e\n          \u003cspan class={styles.DataLabel}\u003ePosition\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003cspan class={styles.DataValue}\u003e\n            {Math.round(cropData().x)}, {Math.round(cropData().y)}\n          \u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.DataItem}\u003e\n          \u003cspan class={styles.DataLabel}\u003eSize\u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003cspan class={styles.DataValue}\u003e\n            {Math.round(cropData().width)} x {Math.round(cropData().height)}\n          \u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nconst cropData = ref({ x: 0, y: 0, width: 0, height: 0 })\nconst zoom = :class=\"styles.Image\"\n          src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n          alt=\"Sample\"\n        /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Selection :class=\"styles.Selection\"\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle\n            v-for=\"position in ImageCropper.handles\"\n            :key=\"position\"\n            :class=\"styles.Handle\"\n            :position=\"position\"\n          \u003e\n            \u003cdiv /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Grid :class=\"styles.Grid\"    \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.DataDisplay\"\u003e\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.DataItem\"\u003e\n        \u003cspan :class=\"styles.DataItem\"\u003e\n        \u003cspan :class=\"styles.DataLabel\"\u003ePosition\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cspan :class=\"styles.DataValue\"\u003e{{ Math.round(cropData.x) }}, {{ Math.round(cropData.y) }}\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.DataItem\"\u003e\n        \u003cspan :class=\"styles.DataLabel\"\u003eSize\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cspan :class=\"styles.DataValue\"\u003e{{ Math.round(cropData.width) }} x {{ Math.round(cropData.height) }}\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/svelte/image-cropper'\n  import styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\n  let cropData = $state({ x: 0, y: 0, width: 0, height: 0 })\n  let zoom = $state(1)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n  \u003cImageCropper.Root\n    class={styles.Root}\n    onCropChange={(e) =\u003e (cropData = e.crop)}\n    onZoomChange={(e) =\u003e (zoom = e.zoom)}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Image\n        class={styles.Image}\n        src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n        alt=\"Sample\"\n      /\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n        {#each ImageCropper.handles as position}\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} {position}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n        {/each}\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\n  \u003cdiv class={styles.DataDisplay}\u003e\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.DataItem}\u003e\n      \u003cspan class={styles.DataLabel}\u003eZoom\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003cspan class={styles.DataValue}\u003e{zoom.toFixed(2)}x\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.DataItem}\u003e\n      \u003cspan class={styles.DataLabel}\u003ePosition\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003cspan class={styles.DataValue}\u003e\n        {Math.round(cropData.x)}, {Math.round(cropData.y)}\n      \u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.DataItem}\u003e\n      \u003cspan class={styles.DataLabel}\u003eSize\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003cspan class={styles.DataValue}\u003e\n        {Math.round(cropData.width)} x {Math.round(cropData.height)}\n      \u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Context\n\nUse `ImageCropper.Context` to access the cropper API from anywhere inside the root. You get methods like `zoomBy`,\n`rotateBy`, and `setZoom`.\n\n**Example: context**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Context\u003e\n          {(context) =\u003e (\n            \u003cdiv className={button.Group}\u003e\n              \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e context.zoomBy(-0.1)}\u003e\n                \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/button\u003e\n              \u003cspan style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', padding: '0 0.5rem', minWidth: '3rem', textAlign: 'center' }}\u003e\n                {context.zoom.toFixed(1)}x\n              \u003c/span\u003e\n              \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e context.zoomBy(0.1)}\u003e\n                \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/button\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Context\u003e\n\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Context\u003e\n          {(context) =\u003e (\n            \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n              \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e context().zoomBy(-0.1)}\u003e\n                \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/button\u003e\n              \u003cspan\n                style={{ 'font-size': '0.875rem', padding: '0 0.5rem', 'min-width': '3rem', 'text-align': 'center' }}\n              \u003e\n                {context().zoom.toFixed(1)}x\n              \u003c/span\u003e\n              \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e context().zoomBy(0.1)}\u003e\n                \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/button\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Context\u003e\n\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            class={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomIn, ZoomOut } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Layout\"\u003e\n    \u003cImageCropper.Root :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Context v-slot=\"context\"\u003e\n        \u003cdiv :class=\"button.Group\"\u003e\n          \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"context.zoomBy(-0.1)\"\u003e\n            \u003cZoomOut /\u003e\n          \u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003cspan :style=\"{ fontSize: '0.875rem', padding: '0 0.5rem', minWidth: '3rem', textAlign: 'center' }\"\u003e\n            {{ context.zoom.toFixed(1) }}x\n          \u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"context.zoomBy(0.1)\"\u003e\n            \u003cZoomIn /\u003e\n          \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Context\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.Viewport :class=\"styles.Viewport\"\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Image\n          :class=\"styles.Image\"\n \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ImageCropper, type UseImageCropperContext } from '@ark-ui/svelte/image-cropper'\n  import { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv \u003c/ImageCropper.Root\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nUse `RootProvider` with `useImageCropper` when you need to control the cropper from outside the component tree. Build\ncustom toolbars or integrate with form state.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ImageCropper, useImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/react/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const imageCropper = useImageCropper()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={button.Group}\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e imageCropper.setZoom(imageCropper.zoom - 0.1)}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cspan style={{ fontSize: '0.875rem', minWidth: '3rem', textAlign: 'center' }}\u003e\n          {imageCropper.zoom.toFixed(1)}x\n        \u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e imageCropper.setZoom(imageCropper.zoom + 0.1)}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={imageCropper}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            className={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection className={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            {ImageCropper.handles.map((position) =\u003e (\n              \u003cImageCropper.Handle className={styles.Handle} key={position} position={position}\u003e\n                \u003cdiv /\u003e\n              \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n            ))}\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid className={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport { ImageCropper, useImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/solid/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const imageCropper = useImageCropper()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv \u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003cspan style={{ 'font-size': '0.875rem', 'min-width': '3rem', 'text-align': 'center' }}\u003e\n          {imageCropper().zoom.toFixed(1)}x\n        \u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e imageCropper().setZoom(imageCropper().zoom + 0.1)}\u003e\n          \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n\n      \u003cImageCropper.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={imageCropper}\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Image\n            class={styles.Image}\n            src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n            alt=\"Sample\"\n          /\u003e\n          \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n            \u003cFor each={ImageCropper.handles}\u003e\n              {(position) =\u003e (\n                \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} position={position}\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv /\u003e\n                \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n            \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n        \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { ImageCropper, useImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/vue/image-cropper'\nimport { ZoomIn, ZoomOut } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\nconst imageCropper = useImageCropper()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Layout\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :class=\"button.Group\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"imageCropper.setZoom(imageCropper.zoom - 0.1)\"\u003e\n        \u003cZoomOut /\u003e\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cspan :style=\"{ fontSize: '0.875rem', minWidth: '3rem', textAlign: 'center' }\"\u003e\n        {{ imageCropper.zoom.toFixed(1) }}x\n      \u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"imageCropper.setZoom(imageCropper.zoom + 0.1)\"\u003e\n        \u003cZoomIn /\u003e\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cImageCropper.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"imageCropper\"\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Viewport :class=\"styles.Viewport\"\u003e\n \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ImageCropper, useImageCropper } from '@ark-ui/svelte/image-cropper'\n  import { ZoomInIcon, ZoomOutIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/image-cropper.module.css'\n\n  const imageCropper = useImageCropper()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class={styles.Layout}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class={button.Group}\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e imageCropper().setZoom(imageCropper().zoom - 0.1)}\u003e\n      \u003cZoomOutIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003cspan style=\"font-size: 0.875rem; min-width: 3rem; text-align: center;\"\u003e\n      {imageCropper().zoom.toFixed(1)}x\n    \u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e imageCropper().setZoom(imageCropper().zoom + 0.1)}\u003e\n      \u003cZoomInIcon /\u003e\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cImageCropper.RootProvider src=\"https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1506905925346-21bda4d32df4?w=800\"\n        alt=\"Sample\"\n      /\u003e\n      \u003cImageCropper.Selection class={styles.Selection}\u003e\n        {#each ImageCropper.handles as position}\n          \u003cImageCropper.Handle class={styles.Handle} {position}\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/ImageCropper.Handle\u003e\n        {/each}\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"horizontal\" /\u003e\n        \u003cImageCropper.Grid class={styles.Grid} axis=\"vertical\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/ImageCropper.Selection\u003e\n    \u003c/ImageCropper.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003c/ImageCropper.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `aspectRatio` | `number` | No | The aspect ratio to maintain for the crop area (width / height).\nFor example, an aspect ratio of 16 / 9 will maintain a width to height ratio of 16:9.\nIf not provided, the crop area can be freely resized. |\n| `cropShape` | `'circle' | 'rectangle'` | No | The shape of the crop area. |\n| `defaultFlip` | `FlipState` | No | The initial flip state to apply to the image. |\n| `defaultRotation` | `number` | No | The initial rotation to apply to the image in degrees. |\n| `defaultZoom` | `number` | No | The initial zoom factor to apply to the image. |\n| `fixedCropArea` | `boolean` | No | Whether the crop area is fixed in size and position. |\n| `flip` | `FlipState` | No | The controlled flip state of the image. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{\n  root: string\n  viewport: string\n  image: string\n  selection: string\n  handle: (position: string) =\u003e string\n}\u003e` | No | The ids of the image cropper elements |\n| `initialCrop` | `Rect` | No | The initial rectangle of the crop area.\nIf not provided, a smart default will be computed based on viewport size and aspect ratio. |\n| `maxHeight` | `number` | No | The maximum height of the crop area |\n| `maxWidth` | `number` | No | The maximum width of the crop area |\n| `maxZoom` | `number` | No | The maximum zoom factor allowed. |\n| `minHeight` | `number` | No | The minimum height of the crop area |\n| `minWidth` | `number` | No | The minimum width of the crop area |\n| `minZoom` | `number` | No | The minimum zoom factor allowed. |\n| `nudgeStep` | `number` | No | The base nudge step for keyboard arrow keys (in pixels). |\n| `nudgeStepCtrl` | `number` | No | The nudge step when Ctrl/Cmd key is held (in pixels). |\n| `nudgeStepShift` | `number` | No | The nudge step when Shift key is held (in pixels). |\n| `onCropChange` | `(details: CropChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Callback fired when the crop area changes. |\n| `onFlipChange` | `(details: FlipChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Callback fired when the flip state changes. |\n| `onRotationChange` | `(details: RotationChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Callback fired when the rotation changes. |\n| `onZoomChange` | `(details: ZoomChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Callback fired when the zoom level changes. |\n| `rotation` | `number` | No | The controlled rotation of the image in degrees (0 - 360). |\n| `translations` | `IntlTranslations` | No | Specifies the localized strings that identify accessibility elements and their states. |\n| `zoom` | `number` | No | The controlled zoom level of the image. |\n| `zoomSensitivity` | `number` | No | Controls how responsive pinch-to-zoom is. |\n| `zoomStep` | `number` | No | |\n\n\n### Context\n\n**API:**\n\n| Property | Type | Description |\n|----------|------|-------------|\n| `zoom` | `number` | The current zoom level of the image. |\n| `rotation` | `number` | The current rotation of the image in degrees. |\n| `flip` | `FlipState` | The current flip state of the image. |\n| `crop` | `Rect` | The current crop area rectangle in viewport coordinates. |\n| `offset` | `Point` | The current offset (pan position) of the image. |\n| `naturalSize` | `Size` | The natural (original) size of the image. |\n| `viewportRect` | `BoundingRect` | The viewport rectangle dimensions and position. |\n| `dragging` | `boolean` | Whether the crop area is currently being dragged. |\n| `panning` | `boolean` | Whether the image is currently being panned. |\n| `setZoom` | `(zoom: number) =\u003e void` | Function to set the zoom level of the image. |\n| `zoomBy` | `(delta: number) =\u003e void` | Function to zoom the image by a relative amount. |\n| `setRotation` | `(rotation: number) =\u003e void` | Function to set the rotation of the image. |\n| `rotateBy` | `(degrees: number) =\u003e void` | Function to rotate the image by a relative amount in degrees. |\n| `setFlip` | `(flip: Partial\u003cFlipState\u003e) =\u003e void` | Function to set the flip state of the image. |\n| `flipHorizontally` | `(value?: boolean) =\u003e void` | Function to flip the image horizontally. Pass a boolean to set explicitly or omit to toggle. |\n| `flipVertically` | `(value?: boolean) =\u003e void` | Function to flip the image vertically. Pass a boolean to set explicitly or omit to toggle. |\n| `resize` | `(handlePosition: HandlePosition, delta: number) =\u003e void` | Function to resize the crop area from a handle programmatically. |\n| `reset` | `() =\u003e void` | Function to reset the cropper to its initial state. |\n| `getCroppedImage` | `(options?: GetCroppedImageOptions) =\u003e Promise\u003cstring | Blob\u003e` | Function to get the cropped image with all transformations applied.\nReturns a Promise that resolves to either a Blob or data URL. |\n| `getCropData` | `() =\u003e CropData` | Function to get the crop data in natural image pixel coordinates.\nThese coordinates are relative to the original image dimensions,\naccounting for zoom, rotation, and flip transformations.\nUse this for server-side cropping or state persistence. |\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"14:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"ref\":\"$undefined\",\"className\":\"pos_relative w_100% max-w_8xl mx_auto px_4 md:px_8 d_flex py_12 gap_8
